function analyticsAddScript(script) {
	var ezDynamic = document.createElement('script');
	ezDynamic.type = 'text/javascript';
	ezDynamic.innerHTML = script;
	document.head.appendChild(ezDynamic);
}
function getCookiesWithPrefix() {
    var allCookies = document.cookie.split(';');
    var cookiesWithPrefix = {};

    for (var i = 0; i < allCookies.length; i++) {
        var cookie = allCookies[i].trim();

        for (var j = 0; j < arguments.length; j++) {
            var prefix = arguments[j];
            if (cookie.indexOf(prefix) === 0) {
                var cookieParts = cookie.split('=');
                var cookieName = cookieParts[0];
                var cookieValue = cookieParts.slice(1).join('=');
                cookiesWithPrefix[cookieName] = decodeURIComponent(cookieValue);
                break; // Once matched, no need to check other prefixes
            }
        }
    }

    return cookiesWithPrefix;
}

</h1> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-09a1fff elementor-blockquote--skin-border elementor-widget elementor-widget-blockquote" data-id="09a1fff" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="blockquote.default"> <blockquote class="elementor-blockquote"> <p class="elementor-blockquote__content">
				Being a busy mom means your energy is pulled in a hundred different directions every day. High-protein meals help keep you full longer, support steady energy levels, and reduce constant snacking between meals. Instead of sugar crashes and quick hunger, protein-rich recipes give your body what it needs to stay focused, strong, and satisfied.

At Naomy’s Kitchen, we focus on simple high-protein recipes that fit real life  quick breakfasts, easy lunches, and comforting dinners that nourish you and your family without adding stress. Because when meals work with your schedule, not against it, taking care of yourself becomes easier.			</p> <div class="e-q-footer"> <cite class="elementor-blockquote__author">Naomy Wells</cite> </div> </blockquote> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-b8b0bc0 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="b8b0bc0" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-be4e38b elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="be4e38b" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Join my free email list to receive THREE free recipes!</h2> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e217376 elementor-button-align-stretch elementor-widget elementor-widget-form" data-id="e217376" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-settings='{"step_next_label":"Next","step_previous_label":"Previous","button_width":"100","step_type":"number_text","step_icon_shape":"circle"}' data-widget_type="form.default"> <form class="elementor-form" method="post" name="New Form" aria-label="New Form"> <input type="hidden" name="post_id" value="1900"> <input type="hidden" name="form_id" value="e217376"> <input type="hidden" name="referer_title" value="Home - naomyskitchen.com"> <input type="hidden" name="queried_id" value="1900"> <div class="elementor-form-fields-wrapper elementor-labels-above"> <div class="elementor-field-type-email elementor-field-group elementor-column elementor-field-group-email elementor-col-100 elementor-field-required"> <label for="form-field-email" class="elementor-field-label">
